SELECT [o].[OrderAppId], [o].[CustomerId], [o].[OrderTime], [o].[ProductId], [o].[SellCount], [t].[Id], [t].[AccessFailedCount], [t].[ConcurrencyStamp], [t].[Discriminator], [t].[Email], [t].[EmailConfirmed], [t].[LockoutEnabled], [t].[LockoutEnd], [t].[NormalizedEmail], [t].[NormalizedUserName], [t].[PasswordHash], [t].[PhoneNumber], [t].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [t].[SecurityStamp], [t].[TwoFactorEnabled], [t].[UserName], [t].[CustomerAddress], [t].[CustomerGender], [t].[CustomerMobile], [t].[CustomerName], [t].[CustomerProfileImage], [t].[CustomerRegisterDate], [p].[ProductId], [p].[ProductDescription], [p].[ProductGroupId], [p].[ProductImage], [p].[ProductName], [p].[ProductPrice], [p].[ProductStatus], [p].[ProductStock]
FROM [OrderApps] AS [o]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[AccessFailedCount], [a].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a].[Discriminator], [a].[Email], [a].[EmailConfirmed], [a].[LockoutEnabled], [a].[LockoutEnd], [a].[NormalizedEmail], [a].[NormalizedUserName], [a].[PasswordHash], [a].[PhoneNumber], [a].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a].[SecurityStamp], [a].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a].[UserName], [a].[CustomerAddress], [a].[CustomerGender], [a].[CustomerMobile], [a].[CustomerName], [a].[CustomerProfileImage], [a].[CustomerRegisterDate]
    FROM [AspNetUsers] AS [a]
    WHERE [a].[Discriminator] = N'Customer'
